---
title: 制作第一个HEXO主题(未完待续)
date: 2017-03-23 20:48:31
categories: Hexo
tags: [hexo, 主题]
urlname: first_homemade_hexo_theme
---

## 文章更新

1. 20170323-初次成文

## 为什么会有这篇文章

可能是觉得Hexo主题都没有适合做CMS的，所以决定自己写一个。

## 寻找主题

这个比较简单，去GOOGLE一搜就有很多响应式的WORDPRESS模板，找一个自己喜欢的，然后把html，图片还有js都down下来。

这里推荐一个工具，[HTML FORMATTER](http://www.freeformatter.com/html-formatter.html)，一般直接看网页的源代码都是没有格式的，用工具格式化之后会方便很多。

选定的网站是https://www.templatemonster.com/wordpress-themes/monstroid/，直接转换之后代码如下

``` html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en-US">
    <head>
        <title>
            Monstroid WordPress Theme #55555
        </title>
        <meta charset="utf-8">

                    <script type="application/javascript">
                        (function () {
                        	function isLocalStorageExists() {
                        		try {
                        			localStorage.setItem('t*',1);
                        			localStorage.removeItem('t*');
                        			return true;
                        		} catch(e) {
                        			return false;
                        		}
                        	}
                        	function getCookie(key) {
                        		var ca = document.cookie.match( '(^|;) ?'+key+'=([^;]*)(;|$)' );
                        		var c=null;
                        		if ( ca ) {if (typeof(ca[2]) != "undefined") { c=ca[2];}}
                        		return c;
                        	}
                        	if (isLocalStorageExists()) {
                        		var avatarData = JSON.parse( localStorage.getItem('avatar') );
                        		if (avatarData && avatarData.cid === getCookie('cid') && getCookie('access_token')) {
                        			var avatar = avatarData.html,
                        					signinMenu = document.getElementById('menu-signin-block'),
                        					accountMenu = document.getElementById('menu-account-block'),
                        					avatarElement = document.getElementById('user-avatar');
                        			if (signinMenu && accountMenu) {
                        				if (avatarElement && avatar) {
                        					avatarElement.outerHTML = avatar;
                        				}
                        				accountMenu.className = accountMenu.className.replace('hidden', '');
                        				signinMenu.className = signinMenu.className + ' hidden';
                        			}
                        		} else {
                        			localStorage.removeItem('avatar');
                        		}
                        	}
                        })();
                    </script>
                    <li class="user-menu-element">
                        <span id="shp-cart" data-target="_blank" data-href="https://www.templatemonster.com/cart.php" class="shop-cart menu-element-inner js-btn link-click">
                        <span class="tm-icon icon-cart"></span>
                        <span class="menu-element-text">Cart</span>
                        <span class="cart-count js-cart-count" id="cart-count">
                        <span></span>
                        </span>
                        </span>
                    </li>
                </ul>
                <span id="ScMail" style="display: none"></span>
                <script type="application/javascript">
                    (function () {
                    	function isLocalStorageExists() {
                    		try {
                    			localStorage.setItem('t*',1);
                    			localStorage.removeItem('t*');
                    			return true;
                    		} catch(e) {
                    			return false;
                    		}
                    	}
                    
                    	if (isLocalStorageExists()) {
                    		var userlogin = localStorage.getItem('userlogin');
                    		if (userlogin) {
                    			var ScMail_div = document.getElementById('ScMail');
                    			if (ScMail_div) {
                    				ScMail_div.innerHTML = userlogin;
                    			}
                    		}
                    	}
                    })();
                </script>
            </div>

                                            <div class="short-description">
                                                <p itemprop="description">Building a site is not an easy task unless you are armed with a multipurpose WordPress theme that can be adjusted to any possible online resource. Here comes Monstroid - a WordPress theme that has everything you ever dreamed about: starting from great number of predefined pages, up to dozen of child themes and 23 built-in plugins that provide extensive customization options. Visual tweaks allow you to make your Monstroid-powered website look unlike anything build previously.</p>

                                                            <div class="yotpo-header yotpo-verified-buyer ">
                                                                <span class="yotpo-icon-profile yotpo-header-element pull-left"> <label class="yotpo-user-letter">C</label> <span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-circle-checkmark yotpo-action-hover" data-type="toggleFade" data-target="yotpo-tool-tip"></span> </span> 
                                                                <div class="yotpo-header-element">
                                                                    <label class="y-label yotpo-user-name yotpo-font-bold pull-left">Carsten S.</label> 
                                                                    <div class="label-with-tooltip pull-left">
                                                                        <span class="y-label yotpo-user-title yotpo-action-hover" data-type="toggleFade" data-target="yotpo-tool-tip">Verified Buyer</span> 
                                                                        <div class="yotpo-tool-tip yotpo-animation-fade" data-user-type="yotpo-verified-buyer">
                                                                            <div class="tool-tip-header"> <span>What is a</span> <span class="header-green">Verified Buyer</span> </div>

                                                                    <span class="yotpo-review-stars"> <span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-star pull-left"></span><span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-star pull-left"></span><span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-star pull-left"></span><span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-star pull-left"></span><span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-star pull-left"></span> </span>

                                                            <div class="yotpo-main">
                                                                <div class="content-title yotpo-font-bold"> Just great </div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-clr"></div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-review-wrapper">
                                                                    <div class="content-review"> This Template is multifunctional with a lot of possibilities - sometimes complex to find a function - but then - it's just great. Gallery, Video, Contact, Parallax - all works just great and responsive. Backend come with monstroid, moto press and cherry framework - if you can work with that - this template is the best for you. A great Bonus and Help is the litte StyleSwitcher. Lot's of Sites are integrated - for almost every Type of Site - and it's Wordpress. </div>

                                                            <div class="yotpo-main">
                                                                <div class="content-title yotpo-font-bold"> MONSTROID Opened a new door in my business </div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-clr"></div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-review-wrapper">
                                                                    <div class="content-review"> I choose MONSTROID for 3 key reasons: <br>1- I get built in MotoPress Page Builder and Slider (29$+19$) without extra pay for lifetime license <br>2- Cherry Framework 4 and many useful plugins integrated (such as White Label) <br>3- Both of WooCommerce and Normal style website available just in one theme <br>I am a Wordpress Freelancer since 2011 with coding skills in PHP, C++, a little CSS and .... I have the lifetime account in Themify and Elegantthemes, but the 1st use of Templatemonster was for shibint.com an international logistic corporation, that was not cherry framework. <br>I choose Templatemonster products for my VIP customers and used these products more times. <br>When I bought MONSTROID for the 1st time I found it very amazing. After 10 days I bought 5 licenses (Developer) again. <br>1st MONSTROID used for mehrtarkhis.com that is Export/Import company, then I used it for another customer and I decided to upgrade all Cherry Framework themes before V4.0 to MONSTROID that it will make easier for support and updates. <br>I used 1 license for demo.buildyourscreen.com that is for preview versions of my customers that can see features of MONSTROID and practice how it works. <br>and another use was for planoforeignauto.com a Car Repair Service in Dallas. <br>I 've forgotten some of these customers that installed MONSTROID (because now I writing this text is 2:30am) <br>I have a personal website m0911.com has blog style and decided to install replace its theme by MONSTROID as soon as possible. <br>Cherry v4 has RTL but I am not sure yet if it is sufficient for MONSTROID or it is necessary adding more CSS for exact RTL but I did my jobs without any problem. <br>I suggest full RTL in next generation of MONSTROID that can make it most popular one time forever. <br>The special flexibility of MONSTROID is changing the theme to one of its child themes in every step of website building that you will not force to pay again. <br>Because of good support that I experienced it (even for easy CSS codes they guided me), I suggest this theme for both of beginner and expert Wordpress Freelancers. <br>The last word ... MONSTROID is 5 STARTS and only 5 STARTS. </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <a href="https://yotpo.com/go/vZwbP1ZR" target="_blank">
                                                                    <div data-product-id="6603751" class="y-label product-link">On Monstroid WordPress Theme #55555</div>
                                                                </a>

                                                            <div class="yotpo-main">
                                                                <div class="content-title yotpo-font-bold"> Монстроид превысил мои ожидания </div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-clr"></div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-review-wrapper">
                                                                    <div class="content-review"> Перед тем как преобрести тему я долго разбирал много других тем на разных движках. Одним из из аргументов почиму я выбрал Монстроид так это функциалность и адаптивность, в своем сайте на этом шаблоне я гармонично отобразил 4 напрвления бизнеса с подвидами услуг а также интернет магазин, для меня это важно я хочу в ходе эксплуатации сайта розширять свои предложения и докручивать. К тому же на движке WordPress я уже работал он для меня понятен и удобен. </div>

                                                                <div class="content-title yotpo-font-bold"> Great WordPress template </div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-clr"></div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-review-wrapper">
                                                                    <div class="content-review"> Great template with a lot of features + bonus Moto Press licence and sub-templates. <br>Very easy to configure, great documentation and best support. <br>Sample content is included, so it is very easy to make look and feel as in template demo page. <br>I like parallax templates and this was best choice of many many templates in WordPress category. </div>

                                                                        <div class="content-question"> A: Please, contact your hosting company and ask them to increase the following values to the provided ones: <br>max_execution_time = 90 <br>max_input_time = 120 <br>memory_limit = 256M <br>post_max_size = 256M <br>upload_max_filesize = 128M <br>You may also check this troubleshooter: https://www.templatemonster.com/help/cherryframework4-and-monstroid-installation-possible-issues-and-solutions.html </div>

                                                                    <div class="yotpo-header yotpo-store-owner ">
                                                                        <span class="yotpo-icon-profile yotpo-header-element yotpo-store-avatar">
                                                                            <div class="yopto-avatar-wrapper"> <img class="yotpo-store-avatar" src="//ddcfq0gxiontw.cloudfront.net/App/23957/12413086/thumb.png?1476954949" alt="TemplateMonster"/> </div>
                                                                            <span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-circle-checkmark yotpo-action-hover" data-type="toggleFade" data-target="yotpo-tool-tip"></span>

                                                                        <div class="yotpo-header-element"> <label class="y-label yotpo-user-name yotpo-font-bold pull-left">TemplateMonster</label> </div>
                                                                        <div class="yotpo-header-element yotpo-header-actions"> <label class="y-label question-date">02/27/17</label> </div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                    <div class="yotpo-main">
                                                                        <div class="content-title yotpo-font-bold"> </div>
                                                                        <div class="content-question"> A: Most of the colors can be changed at the Cherry -&gt; Options section at site admin panel. In certain cases you will also need to add the custom style rules to the Style.css file at the Appearance -&gt; Editor, that file is included to the template especially for your customization purposes. This tutorial will guide you through https://www.templatemonster.com/help/cherryframework-4-how-to-add-custom-css-styles.html </div>

                                                                <div class="yotpo-header-element">

                                                                    <div class="label-with-tooltip pull-left">
                                                                        <span class="y-label yotpo-user-title yotpo-action-hover" data-type="toggleFade" data-target="yotpo-tool-tip">Verified Reviewer</span> 
                                                                        <div class="yotpo-tool-tip yotpo-animation-fade" data-user-type="yotpo-verified-user">
                                                                            <div class="tool-tip-header"> <span>What is a</span> <span class="header-blue">Verified Reviewer</span> </div>

                                                            </div>
                                                            <div class="yotpo-main">
                                                                <div class="content-question yotpo-font-bold"> Q: Where do I get my Motopress plugins' license keys for Monstroid template? </div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-clr"></div>
                                                            </div>
                                                            <div class="yotpo-footer">
                                                                <div class="footer-actions"> <span class="yotpo-action" data-type="toggleFade" data-target=".yotpo-comments-box,.yotpo-show-more"> <span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-chat-bubble y-label"></span> <label class="y-label">Answers (1)</label> </span> </div>
                                                                <div class="yotpo-clr"></div>
                                                            </div>
                                                            <div class="no-border yotpo-comments-box visible">
                                                                <div class="yotpo-comment-box yotpo-comment " data-answer-id="1162012">
                                                                    <div class="yotpo-header yotpo-store-owner ">
                                                                        <span class="yotpo-icon-profile yotpo-header-element yotpo-store-avatar">
                                                                            <div class="yopto-avatar-wrapper"> <img class="yotpo-store-avatar" src="//ddcfq0gxiontw.cloudfront.net/App/23957/12413086/thumb.png?1476954949" alt="TemplateMonster"/> </div>
                                                                            <span class="yotpo-icon yotpo-icon-circle-checkmark yotpo-action-hover" data-type="toggleFade" data-target="yotpo-tool-tip"></span> 
                                                                        </span>
                                                                        <div class="yotpo-header-element"> <label class="y-label yotpo-user-name yotpo-font-bold pull-left">TemplateMonster</label> </div>
                                                                        <div class="yotpo-header-element yotpo-header-actions"> <label class="y-label question-date">02/24/17</label> </div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                    <div class="yotpo-main">
                                                                        <div class="content-title yotpo-font-bold"> </div>
                                                                        <div class="content-question"> A: Visit the http://www.getmotopress.com/my-account/ page and press 'Lost password?' link. Enter the email address you used for the Monstroid theme purchase to the input field and check your Inbox - you will get a message with the password. Use it to login to your MotoPress account and find the license keys at the 'View Details &amp; Downloads' section. </div>
                                                                    </div>

                                                            <th>Changelog:</th>
                                                            <td>
                                                                <span>
                                                                    <b>Monstroid Version 1.1.3 (August 1, 2016):</b><br/>
                                                                    <b>Additions</b>
                                                                    <ul>
                                                                        <li>- 5 new child themes, <a href="http://www.templatemonster.com/wordpress-themes/arch-wordpress-theme-57602.html" target="_blank">Arch</a>, <a href="http://www.templatemonster.com/wordpress-themes/american-politician-wordpress-theme-58658.html" target="_blank">American Politician</a>, <a href="http://www.templatemonster.com/wordpress-themes/58390.html" target="_blank">Giglio</a>, <a href="http://www.templatemonster.com/wordpress-themes/58412.html" target="_blank">Play Games</a>, <a href="http://www.templatemonster.com/wordpress-themes/55966.html" target="_blank">Hang Gliding</a>;</li>
                                                                        <li>- Width of the sidebar in 1/3 and 1/4 ratios;</li>
                                                                        <li>- Customization of text and background colors in Cherry Simple Slider;</li>
                                                                        <li>- Option of AutoPlay in Swiper Carousel;</li>
                                                                        <li>- Possibility to set the text content of "Next / Prev" pagination buttons in Portfolio;</li>
                                                                        <li>- Possibility to set images in an ascending or descending order and filter them by categories (date, name, comments, modified);</li>
                                                                        <li>- Integration of bbPress and All-in-One Event Calendar.</li>
                                                                    </ul>
                                                                </span>
```

1. [制作Hexo主题详细教程（1）](http://blog.geekaholic.cn/2017/02/22/%E5%88%B6%E4%BD%9CHexo%E4%B8%BB%E9%A2%98%E8%AF%A6%E7%BB%86%E6%95%99%E7%A8%8B%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89/)
